Here is a comprehensive technical prompt you can use for a UI/UX designer or an AI development tool to build the dashboard.
Prompt: Woreda Administrative & Political Management Portal
Core Concept:
Create a high-fidelity dashboard for a dual-purpose (Administrative and Political) portal used in Ethiopia. The system manages a hierarchy of Woreda (District) → Hibret (Union/Cluster) → Family → Member. The primary goal is "Information Exchange" through a "Command and Response" loop.
1. Visual Style:
Professional & Clean: Data-heavy but organized using a "Modular Card" layout.
Color Palette: Use a base of neutral grays/whites with high-contrast accent colors (e.g., Deep Blue for Administrative, Forest Green for Political).
Navigation: A persistent sidebar with clear sections for: Hierarchy, Communications (Blog & Tasks), Reporting, Analytics, and System Control.
2. Key Page Designs Needed:
A. The "Astedader" (Woreda Admin) Dashboard:
Overview Stats: Total Members (split by Men/Women), Active Announcements, and Report Submission Rate.
Performance Leaderboard: A ranking of Hibrets based on "Reporting Speed" (Early Bird status) and "Member Participation."
Geographic Heatmap: A map showing meeting locations ("pins") based on active Announcements.
B. The "Announcements & Broadcasts" Modules:
Broadcast Feed: A "Blog-style" scrollable feed for political news with image/video support.
Announcement Center: A task-management interface where admins post meeting directives (What, Where, When). Each task should show a "Progress Bar" (e.g., "15/20 Hibrets Reported").
C. The Hibret Submission Portal (The "Response" Form):
Announcement Linker: A dropdown to "Mention" which Woreda directive this report is for.
Member Checklist: A searchable list of all members in the Hibret to check off attendance.
Uploader Section: Drag-and-drop zones for: 1. Official Files (Any format), 2. Photo/Video Gallery (Proof), 3. Qualitative Notes.
D. Member Profile View (Detail Level):
A card-based layout featuring: Name, FAN Card Number, Member ID, Education (e.g., Management Diploma), Work Experience (10 years), Salary, and Monthly Contribution.
E. Control & Audit Pages:
Logs Page: A table view showing: [Timestamp] | [User] | [Action Taken] | [IP Address].
User Management: A grid to toggle "Privileges" for Woreda vs. Hibret Admins.
3. Functional Requirements to Visualize:
Search & Filter: Deep filtering by Gender, Age, Profession, and Political Role.
Real-time Alerts: A notification bell for "Late Reports" or "Urgent Trend Alerts."
Language Toggle: Support for English and Amharic/Local languages.
How would you like to refine this? We could add a section specifically for exporting these analytics into PDF or Excel reports for high-level officials.





it should be dynamic like every dinamic
11:07 PM
To make this dashboard truly dynamic, the design must focus on real-time data reactivity and state changes. Nothing should be static; every action at the Member level should instantly ripple up to the Woreda-level analytics.
Here is the refined prompt for a Dynamic, State-Driven Dashboard Build:
Technical Prompt: Dynamic Woreda Political-Administrative Engine
System Architecture Goal:
Build a fully dynamic, real-operative portal where the UI reacts instantly to the "Back and Forth" information exchange. The hierarchy is: Woreda (Root) → Hibret (Node) → Family (Cluster) → Member (Individual).
1. Dynamic Data Flow Requirements
Live Propagation: When a Hibret Admin checks a "Member" as present in a meeting, the Woreda’s "Total Attendance" counter and "Gender Split" chart must update via WebSockets/Real-time sync without a page refresh.
The "Mention" Logic: The reporting form must be context-aware. When a user selects a specific "Announcement," the form should dynamically change its fields (e.g., if the announcement is a "Youth Conference," the Member Checklist should automatically filter to show only members under age 30).
Nested Hierarchy Navigation: Use an Expandable Tree View for the Administrative Analytics. Clicking a Woreda opens Hibrets; clicking a Hibret opens Families; clicking a Family reveals the Member Card (Halima’s profile).
2. Component-Specific Dynamic Features
The "Active Directive" Command Center (Woreda View):
Live Progress Rings: Every Announcement shows a circular progress bar that moves in real-time as Hibrets hit "Submit."
Dynamic Flagging: Any report submitted without a "Gallery" (photo/video) or with "Missing Required Fields" should trigger a red pulse on the Woreda’s map.
The Intelligent Reporting Portal (Hibret View):
Multi-Format Previewer: An inline file viewer that allows the Admin to preview PDFs, Word docs, or Videos directly inside the dashboard before final submission.
Auto-Calculated KPI Cards: As the Admin types in the "Notes" or checks "Attendance," a side-panel should show their Performance Score changing dynamically (e.g., "Early Submission Bonus: +10%").
Member Profile "Data-Pill" System:
Member fields (Salary, FAN, Education) should be inline-editable. Changes should trigger an automatic entry in the Logs Page identifying who made the change and what the previous value was.
3. Advanced Analytics & Logs
Dynamic Trend Filtering: A "Political Trend" dashboard where the Woreda Admin can drag a time-slider. As the slider moves, the charts for Sentiment, Grievances, and Participation must morph to reflect that specific time window.
Live Audit Logs: A scrolling vertical feed on the Admin’s sidebar showing a live stream of system activity (e.g., "2 seconds ago: Hibret A linked a report to Announcement #10").
4. UI/UX "Dynamic" Aesthetics
State-Based Theming: The dashboard "vibe" changes based on urgency. If a "High Alert" Announcement is active, the dashboard header glows amber.
Responsive Scaling: The layout must be Mobile-First for Hibret Admins (who are in the field) and Desktop-Optimized for Woreda Admins (who are analyzing data).
Skeleton Loading: Use animated skeleton screens so the UI feels fast while the heavy Member analytics (Gender/Age/Profession) are calculating in the background.
Next Step for the Build:
Should the "Political Trend Report" have a dynamic Sentiment Gauge that automatically moves from "Negative" to "Positive" based on keywords found in the uploaded Notes?





everything in dashboard sould be dynamic more pages and fileds can be added
11:08 PM
This means you need a Schema-Agnostic or Pluggable Architecture. The system shouldn't just display data; it should be a "Dashboard Builder" where the Woreda Admin can evolve the political and administrative structure on the fly.
Here is the technical prompt for a Fully Extensible & Dynamic System Build:
Prompt: The "Living" Woreda Portal (Fully Dynamic Architecture)
The Goal:
Build a meta-dashboard where the hierarchy, data fields, and pages are not hard-coded. The system must allow the Main Admin to add new levels to the administration or new tracking fields to the members without writing new code.
1. Dynamic Schema & Custom Fields:
No-Code Field Creator: The Admin can add new fields to the Member Profile at any time (e.g., adding "Vaccination Status" or "Volunteer Skills").
Instant UI Propagation: Once a field is added, it must automatically appear in the Member Registration Form, the Hibret Checklist, and the Analytics Filter without a system reboot.
Dynamic Data Types: Support for text, numbers, dates, GPS coordinates, and multi-file attachments.
2. Pluggable Page & Module Builder:
Dynamic Routing: The Main Admin can create "New Pages" (e.g., a specific page for "Youth League Development").
Widget-Based Layout: Pages are built using a Drag-and-Drop Grid. Admins can drop "Attendance Charts," "Live Video Feeds," or "Note Aggregators" onto any new page.
Role-Based Visibility: Every new page or field created must have a toggle to define who sees it (Woreda only, Hibret only, or Public).
3. The "Infinite" Information Exchange (Back and Forth):
Custom Report Templates: The Woreda can create a new "Announcement Type." When they do, they define exactly what the "Response" should look like (e.g., "For this specific meeting, I need a CSV upload AND a 30-second video").
Dynamic Linking: The system must allow reports to be linked to multiple announcements or even cross-referenced between different Hibrets.
4. Recursive Hierarchy (The Tree):
The system should not be limited to 3 levels. If the Woreda wants to add a "Sub-Hibret" or "Block Leader" level between the Hibret and the Family, the User Management and Logs must automatically adapt to the new branch.
5. Advanced Dynamic Logs:
Schema Change Logs: Every time a new field or page is added, the Logs Page must record the "Structure Change" so the history of how the dashboard evolved is preserved.
6. Automated Analytics Generation:
Auto-Pivot Tables: Since fields are dynamic, the Analytics engine must be "Smart." If a new "Gender" category or "Profession" is added, the Dashboard Charts must automatically include that new data point in the percentages without manual configuration.
How do you want to handle the "Templates"? Should the Woreda have a set of pre-made dynamic pages they can just "Turn On," or do you want them to build every single page from scratch?

This prompt is designed for Figma AI or a professional UI/UX designer. It focuses on the "Living Dashboard" concept where every element is modular and extensible.
Figma Design Prompt: The "Dynamic Woreda" Governance Engine
Concept:
Design a high-fidelity, hyper-dynamic Enterprise SaaS Dashboard for a regional government hierarchy (Woreda → Hibret → Family → Member). The UI must feel like a "Command Center" where the administration is managed through a live information exchange loop.
1. Layout & Navigation (The Framework):
Modular Sidebar: A collapsible navigation menu using a "Tree Structure" to show the administrative hierarchy.
Global Search Bar: A "Command K" style search at the top that can find any Member (by Name or FAN ID), Announcement, or File across the entire district.
Workspace Canvas: A main stage area that uses a Widget-based Grid system (similar to Notion or Jira) where pages can be built by adding "Blocks."
2. Key Page Templates to Design:
Template A: The "Super-Admin" Control Center
Dynamic Analytics Cards: Modular tiles showing real-time counters for Total Members, Men/Women percentages, and Active Announcements.
Activity Heatmap: A visual matrix showing which Hibrets are "Green" (Active/Early) vs "Red" (Inactive/Late).
Live Stream Feed: A sidebar widget showing the most recent Notes and Media Uploads as they arrive from the field.
Template B: The "Announcement & Broadcast" Engine
Split View: Left side is the Broadcast Feed (Blog-style cards with rich media). Right side is the Announcement Manager (Task-style list with "Deadline" countdowns and "Submission Status" badges).
Action Button: A prominent "Create New Action" button that opens a modal to build custom fields for a specific meeting.
Template C: The Hibret "Reporting Portal" (Mobile-Responsive)
Linking Logic: A prominent header showing which Announcement is currently being responded to.
Smart Checklist: A dynamic list of Member profiles with "One-Tap" attendance toggles.
The "Proof" Tray: A drag-and-drop zone for multiple file formats, a photo/video gallery previewer, and a rich-text editor for Notes.
Template D: The 360° Member Profile (Halima’s View)
Data Grid: A clean list of user fields (FAN Card, ID, Education, Work Exp, Salary).
"Add Field" Placeholder: A dotted-line button at the bottom of the profile that says "+ Add Custom Field" to show the system is dynamic.
Activity Timeline: A vertical line showing every meeting this member has attended and every note written about them.
3. System Components (The UI Kit):
States: Design "Empty States," "Loading States (Skeletons)," and "Success/Error States" for every report submission.
Audit Logs: A dedicated "Log Table" component with filters for User, Action, and Timestamp.
Typography: Use a clean, modern Sans-Serif (like Inter or Roboto) for high readability in both English and Amharic.
Icons: Use a functional icon set (e.g., Lucide or Phosphor) to represent "Meetings," "Trends," "Family," and "Analytics."
4. The "Dynamic" Interaction (The X-Factor):
Incorporate a "Field Builder" interface where an admin can create a new data point (e.g., "Monthly Contribution") and show it instantly appearing across all member cards in the design.
How would you like the first prototype to look? Should we start with the Dark Mode "Operations" look or a Light Mode "Administrative" look?





Ask anything

## The Hierarchy (4 Levels)
1. **Woreda** (District) - Top administrative level
2. **Hibret** (Union/Association) - Middle organizing cluster
3. **Family** (Household) - Base unit
4. **Member** (Individual) - Individual citizen with detailed profile

## Two Portal Types
- **Administrative**: People management, demographics, hierarchy
- **Political**: Meetings, conferences, trend reports, mobilization

1. **Top-down**: Woreda creates Announcements → Broadcasts to Hibrets
2. **Bottom-up**: Hibrets conduct meetings → Submit reports with attendance, photos/videos, notes

| Feature | Purpose |
|---------|---------|
| **Broadcasts** | Blog-style news/updates (one-way) |

| **Political Trend Reports** | Sentiment analysis, grievances, risks |
| **Performance Analytics** | Hibret rankings, attendance stats, early/late submissions |
| **Audit Logs** | Track every action (who did what when) |
| **User Management** | Role-based privileges |

- Contact: Phone, email, zone, woreda, kebele
- IDs: FAN Card, Member ID
- Education: Level, field
- Work: Status, experience years, monthly salary, workplace
- Party: Role, membership year, monthly contribution

- **System Admin**: Full control, user management, logs
- **Woreda Admin**: Create announcements/broadcasts, view all analytics
- **Hibret Admin**: Submit reports, manage families in their hibret only
- **Data Clerk**: Update member profiles only
- **Member**: View-only access

### Planner Response

Based on all the context you've provided, here's what I understand about **Astedader Woreda**:

## What It Is
A **Political-Administrative Portal** for managing Ethiopia's district (Woreda) governance system. It bridges the gap between high-level administration and grassroots political mobilization.

## The Hierarchy (4 Levels)
1. **Woreda** - The district administration (top level)
2. **Hibret** - Unions/associations under the woreda
3. **Family** - Households within each hibret  
4. **Member** - Individual citizens with detailed profiles

## The Core Concept: "Information Exchange"
A **two-way command-response loop**:
- **Top-down**: Woreda sends Broadcasts (news) and Announcements (tasks/orders)
- **Bottom-up**: Hibrets submit Reports with proof (attendance, photos, documents, notes)

## The Two Portals

**Administrative Side** - People management
- View/manage members across all levels
- Demographics, contact info, work details
- Analytics on participation

**Political Side** - Engagement & mobilization
- **Meetings**: Schedule, conduct, report attendance
- **Conferences**: Larger events with delegates
- **Political Trend Reports**: Sentiment, grievances, risks
- **Broadcasts**: One-way news/updates
- **Announcements**: Directives requiring response

## Key Workflows
1. Woreda creates announcement → "Conduct meeting on X date at Y location"
2. Hibret admin sees it → Conducts the meeting
3. Hibret submits report → Attendance list (men/women count), photos, documents, notes
4. Woreda views analytics → Performance rankings, participation rates, response speed

## Roles
- **Super Admin**: Full system control, user management, audit logs
- **Woreda Admin**: Creates announcements/broadcasts, views all analytics
- **Hibret Admin**: Manages their specific hibret, submits reports
- **Regular User/Member**: View access based on privileges

## Member Profile (Detailed)
Includes: FAN Card, personal info, education, work experience, salary, party role, monthly contribution, attendance history.

Is this understanding correct? What would you like me to build next?

### Planner Response

Here's my **final understanding** of the Astedader Woreda system:

## Hierarchy (4 Levels - Strict Top-Down)

1. **Woreda** - District administration, creates announcements/broadcasts, views all analytics
2. **Hibret** - Union/association, manages families, reviews reports, submits to Woreda
3. **Family** - Political group/cell (NOT household), manages members, conducts meetings, submits reports to Hibret
4. **Member** - Individual citizen, views own profile, requests edits, participates

## Information Flow (No Skipping)

**Top-Down Command:**
Woreda → Announcement → Hibret → Family

**Bottom-Up Response:**
Family → Report → Hibret (consolidates) → Woreda

## Two Portals

**Administrative:**
- People management, hierarchy
- Member profiles (FAN Card, education, work, salary, party role)
- Profile edit requests (Member → Family/Hibret → approval)
- Form filling integration

**Political:**
- **Broadcasts** - Blog-style news (one-way)
- **Announcements** - Task directives (require response)
- **Reports** - Linked to announcements, with attendance, photos, videos, documents, notes
- **Political Trend Reports** - Sentiment, grievances, risks
- **Performance Analytics** - Rankings, participation rates, response speed

## Roles & Granular Privileges

| Role | Scope |
|------|-------|
| Super Admin | Full system, user management, audit logs |
| Woreda Admin | Create announcements/broadcasts, view all analytics |
| Hibret Admin | Manage families, review family reports, submit to Woreda |
| Family Admin | Manage members, conduct meetings, submit reports |
| Member | View own profile, request edits, participate |

**Privileges:** `view_members`, `upload_files`, `write_reports`, `manage_meetings`, `manage_conferences`, `submit_trends`, `view_broadcasts`, `chat_access`, `member_management` 

## Key Features

- **Audit Logs** - Track every click/action, timestamped, daily activity per user
- **Chat** - Admin↔Hibret↔Member (same level only, Admin can reach anyone)
- **File Upload** - Excel bulk import, pre-upload preview, archive functionality
- **Broadcast System** - Selective targeting (specific hibrets/members, toggles UI)

Is this correct? Ready to build?

| Who | Can Chat With |

| Hibret Admin | Woreda Admin + Members in their Hibret |
| Member | Hibret Admin + Woreda Admin (direct) |

**Not allowed:** Member ↔ Member (same hibret or different), Hibret Admin ↔ Hibret Admin (different hibrets)

Here's my final understanding of the Astedader Woreda system:

Hierarchy (4 Levels - Strict Top-Down)
Woreda - District administration, creates announcements/broadcasts, views all analytics
Hibret - Union/association, manages families, reviews reports, submits to Woreda
Family - Political group/cell (NOT household), manages members, conducts meetings, submits reports to Hibret
Member - Individual citizen, views own profile, requests edits, participates
Information Flow (No Skipping)
Top-Down Command: Woreda → Announcement → Hibret → Family

Bottom-Up Response: Family → Report → Hibret (consolidates) → Woreda

Two Portals
Administrative:

People management, hierarchy
Member profiles (FAN Card, education, work, salary, party role)
Profile edit requests (Member → Family/Hibret → approval)
Form filling integration
Political:

Broadcasts - Blog-style news (one-way)
Announcements - Task directives (require response)
Reports - Linked to announcements, with attendance, photos, videos, documents, notes
Political Trend Reports - Sentiment, grievances, risks
Performance Analytics - Rankings, participation rates, response speed
Roles & Granular Privileges
Role	Scope
Super Admin	Full system, user management, audit logs
Woreda Admin	Create announcements/broadcasts, view all analytics
Hibret Admin	Manage families, review family reports, submit to Woreda
Family Admin	Manage members, conduct meetings, submit reports
Member	View own profile, request edits, participate

Audit Logs - Track every click/action, timestamped, daily activity per user
Chat - Admin↔Hibret↔Member (same level only, Admin can reach anyone)
File Upload - Excel bulk import, pre-upload preview, archive functionality
Broadcast System - Selective targeting (specific hibrets/members, toggles UI)
Is this correct? Ready to build?

the broadcast should work for the hibrets also the hibrets can send broadcasts

Got it. Broadcasts are bidirectional (hierarchical):

Woreda Admin → can broadcast to all Hibrets OR selective Hibrets
Hibret Admin → can broadcast to their Families/Members
So Hibrets have their own internal communication channel downward, while also receiving from Woreda above.

Level	Can Broadcast To
Woreda Admin	Hibrets (all or selective)
Hibret Admin	Families/Members in their Hibret

the woreda can repost the hibret broadcast

Got it. Amplification/Repost feature:

Hibret creates broadcast → goes to their Families/Members
Woreda Admin sees Hibret broadcast → can repost it to:
Other Hibrets
All Hibrets in the Woreda
So Woreda can amplify Hibret messages upward/outward to broader audience.

Is this correct?

Feedback submitted



okay also messaging chat

Got it. Chat/Messaging is bidirectional (within hierarchy boundaries):

Who	Can Chat With
Woreda Admin	Hibret Admins (multiple) + Any Member (direct)
Hibret Admin	Woreda Admin + Members in their Hibret
Member	Hibret Admin + Woreda Admin (direct)
Not allowed: Member ↔ Member (same hibret or different), Hibret Admin ↔ Hibret Admin (different hibrets)

Is this correct?

Feedback submitted



okay so the pages in each role explain

Here are the pages for each role:

Super Admin (System Level)
Page	Purpose
Dashboard	System overview: total users, woredas, hibrets, activity stats
User Management	Create/edit users, assign roles, set granular privileges
Woredas	Create/manage woredas, assign admins
Audit Logs	View all system actions, timestamps, filter by user/action
Broadcasts	Send system-wide messages, view all broadcasts
Settings	System configuration, custom fields, form templates
Analytics	Cross-woreda statistics, system-wide reports
Woreda Admin (District Level)
Page	Purpose
Dashboard	Woreda overview: hibrets count, members, active announcements, submission rates
Hibrets	View all hibrets in woreda, create new hibrets, assign hibret admins
Families	View families across all hibrets
Members	Full member directory, search/filter, edit profiles
Broadcasts	Create broadcasts to all/selective hibrets, repost hibret broadcasts
Announcements	Create task directives (meetings, conferences, trend reports)
Reports	View submitted reports from hibrets, review attendance, download files
Analytics	Hibret performance rankings, participation rates, response speed
Political Trends	View trend reports, sentiment analysis, grievance tracking
Chat	Message hibret admins, direct message any member
Audit Logs	View activity within their woreda
Hibret Admin (Union Level)
Page	Purpose
Dashboard	Hibret overview: families count, members, pending announcements, report status
Families	Manage families in their hibret, create new families, assign family admins
Members	View/edit members in their hibret, approve profile edit requests
Broadcasts	Create broadcasts to their families/members, view woreda broadcasts
Announcements	View woreda announcements, assign to families
Reports	View family reports, submit consolidated report to woreda
Meeting Reports	Create meeting reports: register attendees, upload photos/documents, add notes
Conference Reports	Same as meetings for conferences
Political Trend Reports	Create and submit trend reports
Chat	Message woreda admin, message members in their hibret
Analytics	Family performance within their hibret
Family Admin (Group Level)
Page	Purpose
Dashboard	Family overview: member count, pending tasks, report status
Members	Manage members in their family, view profiles
Announcements	View hibret-assigned announcements
Reports	Submit reports to hibret (attendance, photos, documents, notes)
Profile Edit Requests	Approve/reject member profile edit requests
Chat	Message hibret admin, message members in their family
Broadcasts	View hibret broadcasts (read-only)
Member (Individual Level)
Page	Purpose
Dashboard	Personal overview: upcoming meetings, unread broadcasts, report status
My Profile	View full profile: FAN Card, education, work, salary, attendance history
Edit Profile	Request edits (phone, email, etc.) → goes to Family/Hibret for approval
Announcements	View announcements assigned to their family/hibret
Reports	View reports they've been included in
Attendance	View their meeting/conference attendance history
Broadcasts	View woreda and hibret broadcasts (read-only)
Chat	Message hibret admin, message woreda admin (direct)
Is this complete? Anything missing or needs adjustment?

Here are the pages for each role:

Super Admin (System Level)
Page	Purpose
Dashboard	System overview: total users, woredas, hibrets, activity stats
User Management	Create/edit users, assign roles, set granular privileges
Woredas	Create/manage woredas, assign admins
Audit Logs	View all system actions, timestamps, filter by user/action
Broadcasts	Send system-wide messages, view all broadcasts
Settings	System configuration, custom fields, form templates
Analytics	Cross-woreda statistics, system-wide reports
Woreda Admin (District Level)
Page	Purpose
Dashboard	Woreda overview: hibrets count, members, active announcements, submission rates
Hibrets	View all hibrets in woreda, create new hibrets, assign hibret admins
Families	View families across all hibrets
Members	Full member directory, search/filter, edit profiles
Broadcasts	Create broadcasts to all/selective hibrets, repost hibret broadcasts
Announcements	Create task directives (meetings, conferences, trend reports)
Reports	View submitted reports from hibrets, review attendance, download files
Analytics	Hibret performance rankings, participation rates, response speed
Political Trends	View trend reports, sentiment analysis, grievance tracking
Chat	Message hibret admins, direct message any member
Audit Logs	View activity within their woreda
Hibret Admin (Union Level)
Page	Purpose
Dashboard	Hibret overview: families count, members, pending announcements, report status
Families	Manage families in their hibret, create new families, assign family admins
Members	View/edit members in their hibret, approve profile edit requests
Broadcasts	Create broadcasts to their families/members, view woreda broadcasts
Announcements	View woreda announcements, assign to families
Reports	View family reports, submit consolidated report to woreda
Meeting Reports	Create meeting reports: register attendees, upload photos/documents, add notes
Conference Reports	Same as meetings for conferences
Political Trend Reports	Create and submit trend reports
Chat	Message woreda admin, message members in their hibret
Analytics	Family performance within their hibret
Family Admin (Group Level)
Page	Purpose
Dashboard	Family overview: member count, pending tasks, report status
Members	Manage members in their family, view profiles
Announcements	View hibret-assigned announcements
Reports	Submit reports to hibret (attendance, photos, documents, notes)
Profile Edit Requests	Approve/reject member profile edit requests
Chat	Message hibret admin, message members in their family
Broadcasts	View hibret broadcasts (read-only)
Member (Individual Level)
Page	Purpose
Dashboard	Personal overview: upcoming meetings, unread broadcasts, report status
My Profile	View full profile: FAN Card, education, work, salary, attendance history
Edit Profile	Request edits (phone, email, etc.) → goes to Family/Hibret for approval
Announcements	View announcements assigned to their family/hibret
Reports	View reports they've been included in
Attendance	View their meeting/conference attendance history
Broadcasts	View woreda and hibret broadcasts (read-only)
Chat	Message hibret admin, message woreda admin (direct)
Is this complete? Anything missing or needs adjustment?

### Planner Response

Here's my **final understanding**:

## **Roles**
1. **Woreda Admin** - Top authority, creates announcements/broadcasts
2. **Hibret Admin** - Manages families, reviews family reports, submits to Woreda
3. **Family Admin** - Manages family members, submits reports to Hibret
4. **Member** - Views profile, requests edits, participates

## **Information Flow**
- **Top-down**: Woreda → Announcement → Hibret → Family
- **Bottom-up**: Family → Report → Hibret → Woreda

## **Woreda Admin Pages**

| Page | Purpose |
|------|---------|
| **Dashboard** | Woreda stats, performance rankings |
| **Hibrets** | Row list → click → Political/Administrative tabs |
| **Members** | Full directory, search/filter by FAN |
| **Broadcasts** | Create to all/selective hibrets, **repost** hibret broadcasts upward |
| **Announcements** | Create meeting/conference/trend directives |
| **Reports Review** | View submitted reports from hibrets |
| **Political Trends** | **View-only** - see all trend reports from hibrets |
| **Analytics** | **Performance only**: Hibret leaderboard, participation rates, response speed |
| **Chat** | Message hibret admins, direct message any member |
| **Audit Logs** | View all woreda activity |
| **Forms** | Create custom form templates |

## **Inside Hibret Detail**

**Political Tab:**
- Meetings
- Conferences  
- Political Trend Reports (**create/submit** here)

**Administrative Tab:**
- Families (list)
- Members in this hibret
- Hibret Admin info
- **Analytics**: Demographics with **default 7 fields** (Gender, Age, Education Level, Education Field, Work Status, Work Experience, Health Status) - **but user can customize and analyze any field**

## **Other Key Features**
- **Member Profile Edit**: Member requests → Family/Hibret approves
- **Chat**: Woreda↔Hibret, Hibret↔Member, Woreda↔Member (direct)
- **Profile Fields** (no excluded fields in data model, just in default analytics view)

Is this correct?

### User Input

Got it. So:

## **Political Trends** moves inside **Hibret detail → Political tab** (not a standalone page)

## **New Page: Gallery**
- Shows all media (photos, videos, documents) from all reports across all hibrets
- Each item shows **source** (which hibret/family it came from)
- Filterable by date, type, hibret

## **Updated Woreda Admin Pages**

| Page | Purpose |
|------|---------|
| **Dashboard** | Woreda stats |
| **Hibrets** | Row list → click → Political/Administrative tabs |
| **Members** | Full directory |
| **Broadcasts** | Create/repost broadcasts |
| **Announcements** | Create directives |
| **Reports Review** | View submitted reports |
| **Analytics** | Performance only (leaderboard) |
| **Chat** | Messaging |
| **Audit Logs** | Activity tracking |
| **Forms** | Create custom forms |
| **Gallery** | All media with source info |

## **Inside Hibret Detail → Political Tab**
- Meetings
- Conferences  
- Political Trend Reports (**create/submit by Hibret**)
- Political Trends (**view trend reports from this hibret**)

Not just viewing submitted reports from Hibrets - it's a **query and generate** tool.

so overall understanding what is your understanding of the asteader woreda admin

### Planner Response

Here's my **comprehensive understanding** of the **Astedader Woreda** system:

---

## **What It Is**
A **dual-purpose Political-Administrative Portal** for Ethiopian district governance. It bridges high-level administration with grassroots political mobilization through a strict hierarchical structure.

---

## **The Hierarchy (4 Levels - No Skipping)**
1. **Woreda** (District) - Astedader Woreda Admin
2. **Hibret** (Union/Association) - Political groups under Woreda
3. **Family** (Political Group/Cell) - NOT household, organizational units under Hibret
4. **Member** (Individual Citizen)

---

## **Information Flow**
**Top-Down Command:** Woreda → Announcement → Hibret → Family
**Bottom-Up Response:** Family → Report → Hibret (consolidates) → Woreda

---

## **Woreda Admin Pages**

| Page | Purpose |
|------|---------|
| **Dashboard** | Overview: hibrets count, members, active announcements, submission rates, performance rankings |
| **Hibrets** | Row list of all hibrets → click opens detail with **Political** & **Administrative** tabs |
| **Members** | Full member directory, search/filter by FAN/ID, edit profiles |
| **Broadcasts** | Create to all/selective hibrets, **repost** hibret broadcasts upward |
| **Announcements** | Create meeting/conference/trend directives with deadlines |
| **Reports** | **Generate custom reports** (query, filter, export PDF/Excel) - general or hibret-specific |
| **Analytics** | **Performance only**: Hibret leaderboard, participation rates, response speed |
| **Chat** | Message hibret admins, direct message any member |
| **Audit Logs** | View all activity within woreda |
| **Forms** | Create custom form templates |
| **Gallery** | All media (photos, videos, documents) from all reports with **source info** |

---

## **Inside Hibret Detail**

### **Political Tab**
- Meetings
- Conferences
- **Political Trend Reports** - Hibret submits, Woreda Admin reviews

### **Administrative Tab**
- Families (list)
- Members in this hibret
- Hibret Admin info
- **Analytics** - Demographics with **default 7 fields**:
  - Gender
  - Age
  - Education Level
  - Education Field
  - Work Status
  - Work Experience
  - Health Status
  - *(But user can customize and analyze ANY field)*

---

## **Key Features**
- **Broadcasts**: Woreda→Hibrets (selective), Hibret→Families, Woreda can **repost** hibret broadcasts upward
- **Reports**: Linked to announcements, with attendance, photos, videos, documents, notes
- **Media Gallery**: All uploaded files with source tracking
- **Profile Edit Requests**: Member requests → Family/Hibret approves
- **Chat**: Woreda↔Hibret, Hibret↔Member, Woreda↔Member (direct)
- **Audit Logs**: Every action timestamped
- **Customizable Analytics**: Default 7 fields, but admin can analyze any profile field

---

## **Privileges (Granular)**
- `view_members` 
- `upload_files` 
- `write_reports` 
- `manage_meetings` 
- `manage_conferences` 
- `submit_trends` 
- `view_broadcasts` 
- `chat_access` 
- `member_management`

### Planner Response

Let me explain the **Reports workflow** clearly:

## **The Command-Response Loop**

**Step 1: Woreda Creates Announcement**
- Woreda Admin goes to **Announcements** page
- Creates: *"Conduct meeting on [Date] at [Location] about [Topic]"*
- Sets deadline for report submission
- Sends to specific Hibrets (or all)

**Step 2: Hibret/Family Executes**
- Hibret Admin sees the announcement in their dashboard
- Conducts the meeting with Families/Members
- Collects attendance, takes photos, records notes

**Step 3: Hibret Submits Report (LINKED to Announcement)**
- Hibret Admin clicks "Submit Report" on that specific announcement
- The report is **automatically linked** to the announcement
- Report contains:
  - **Attendance**: List of who attended (men/women count)
  - **Photos**: Images from the meeting
  - **Videos**: Short clips of speeches/discussions
  - **Documents**: Agendas, minutes, sign-in sheets
  - **Notes**: Written summary of what was discussed

**Step 4: Woreda Reviews**
- Woreda Admin sees the linked report in **Reports** page
- Can view/download all attachments
- Reviews attendance vs expected
- Adds review notes if needed
- Approves or requests resubmission

## **Key Point: The LINK**

The report is **not standalone** - it's always a **response to a specific announcement**:

```
Announcement: "Have meeting about water issues by Friday"
      ↓
Report: "We had the meeting, 45 people attended (25M/20F), 
        here are photos, here are notes about what they said"
```

This creates a **complete audit trail** - Woreda can see:
- What was requested
- What was delivered
- When it was delivered
- Proof it happened

Does this help clarify?

Got it. So the **Reports page** is **Analytics on Reports** - not downloading files.

It shows:
- **Report Strength Score**: How well-organized is it? (completeness, structure, quality)
- **Submission Analytics**: Early vs late, detailed vs minimal
- **Hibret Performance in Reporting**: Which hibrets write good reports vs poor reports
- **Content Analysis**: What topics are most reported, sentiment trends
- **Attachment Quality**: Photo/video quality, document completeness

The actual file downloads happen in the **Gallery** page or inside the **Hibret detail → Political tab**.

### Planner Response

Got it. So the **Reports page** is:

## **Report Analytics & Generation**

**1. Submission Analytics**
- **Attachment Checklist**: Did they submit all required items?
  - Photos: ✓ / ✗
  - Videos: ✓ / ✗
  - Documents: ✓ / ✗
  - Attendance list: ✓ / ✗
  - Notes: ✓ / ✗
- **Completion Rate**: % of hibrets that submitted all required attachments
- **Timeliness**: Early, On-time, Late submissions

**2. Report Generation**
- Generate **overall member detail reports** (demographics, statistics)
- Export as PDF/Excel
- Filter by hibret, date range, announcement type

**NOT about:**
- Quality of content (well-written or not)
- Judgment on organization

**Just facts:**
- Was it submitted?
- Were all attachments included?
- When was it submitted?

## **Reports Page (Analytics + Generation)**

### **1. Submission Analytics**
Checklist for each report:
| Attachment | Status |
|-----------|--------|
| Photos | ✓ Submitted / ✗ Missing |
| Videos | ✓ Submitted / ✗ Missing |
| Documents | ✓ Submitted / ✗ Missing |
| Attendance List | ✓ Submitted / ✗ Missing |
| Notes | ✓ Submitted / ✗ Missing |

**Metrics:**
- **Completion Rate**: % of reports with ALL required attachments
- **Timeliness**: Early, On-time, Late submissions
- **By Hibret**: Which hibrets always complete vs which miss items

### **2. Report Generation**
- **Member Detail Reports**: Overall demographics, statistics
- **Filters**: Hibret, Date range, Announcement type
- **Export**: PDF, Excel

### Planner Response

# **Final Overall Plan - Astedader Woreda Portal**

## **1. Hierarchy (4 Levels)**
```
Woreda (District)
    ↓
Hibret (Political Union/Association)
    ↓
Family (Political Group/Cell - NOT household)
    ↓
Member (Individual)
```

## **2. Information Flow**
- **Top-Down**: Announcements → Hibret → Family
- **Bottom-Up**: Reports → Hibret → Woreda

## **3. Roles**
| Role | Level |
|------|-------|
| **Woreda Admin** | Top authority |
| **Hibret Admin** | Manages families |
| **Family Admin** | Manages members |
| **Member** | Individual user |

## **4. Woreda Admin Pages**

| Page | Purpose |
|------|---------|
| **Dashboard** | Woreda stats, performance rankings |
| **Hibrets** | Row list → click → Political/Administrative tabs |
| **Members** | Full directory, search by FAN |
| **Broadcasts** | Create/repost broadcasts |
| **Announcements** | Create meeting/conference directives |
| **Reports** | **Submission analytics** + Generate member reports |
| **Analytics** | **Performance only**: Leaderboard, participation, response speed |
| **Gallery** | All media with source info |
| **Chat** | Messaging |
| **Audit Logs** | Activity tracking |
| **Forms** | Create custom forms |

## **5. Inside Hibret Detail**

**Political Tab:**
- Meetings
- Conferences  
- Political Trend Reports (Hibret submits → Woreda reviews)

**Administrative Tab:**
- Families (list)
- Members
- Hibret Admin info
- **Analytics**: Demographics (default 7 fields: Gender, Age, Education Level, Education Field, Work Status, Work Experience, Health Status) - **user can customize**

## **6. Key Features**
- **Linked Reports**: Reports linked to announcements
- **Gallery**: All media from reports with source tracking
- **Repost**: Woreda can repost hibret broadcasts upward
- **Chat**: Woreda↔Hibret, Hibret↔Member, Woreda↔Member direct
- **Profile Edit**: Member requests → Family/Hibret approves
- **Customizable Analytics**: Default 7 fields, admin can analyze any field

---

### Planner Response

Got it. So the structure expands:

## **Updated Understanding**

### **Meetings & Conferences**
- **Hibret level**: Hibret conducts meetings with families
- **Family level**: Family conducts meetings with members
- Both can submit reports upward

### **Assignment Types (Announcements)**
Beyond the 3 main types (Meetings, Conferences, Political Trends), there's an **"Others"** category:

| Type | Description |
|------|-------------|
| **Meetings** | Standard meetings |
| **Conferences** | Larger gatherings |
| **Political Trends** | Trend reports |
| **Others** | Unique requests, custom assignments, special tasks |

### **Flow Examples**
```
Woreda → "Others: Conduct survey on water access" → Hibret
Hibret → "Others: Register youth volunteers" → Family
Family → Report back on the unique assignment
```

### **Inside Hibret Detail → Political Tab**
- Meetings (Hibret & Family levels)
- Conferences (Hibret & Family levels)
- Political Trend Reports
- **Others** (unique requests, custom assignments)

Is this correct?
